-- Creating schema and table for customer_feedbacks
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS people;
USE SCHEMA people;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE customer_feedbacks (
  feedback_id INT,
  ticket_id INT,
  rating INT,
  comments STRING,
  feedback_date DATE,
  would_recommend STRING,
  felt_scared BOOLEAN,
  worth_the_price BOOLEAN,
  reviewer_name STRING,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP
);

-- Creating schema and table for haunted_houses
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS attractions;
USE SCHEMA attractions;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE haunted_houses (
  haunted_house_id INT,
  house_name STRING,
  park_area STRING,
  theme STRING,
  fear_level INT,
  house_size_sqft INT,
  duration_minutes INT,
  max_capacity_per_group INT,
  accessibility_friendly STRING,
  min_age_requirement INT,
  opening_year INT,
  house_status STRING,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP
);

-- Creating schema and table for haunted_house_tickets
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS attractions;
USE SCHEMA attractions;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE haunted_house_tickets (
  ticket_id INT,
  customer_id INT,
  haunted_house_id INT,
  purchase_date DATE,
  purchase_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  visit_date DATE,
  visit_hour INT,
  ticket_type STRING,
  ticket_price FLOAT,
  purchase_channel STRING,
  payment_method STRING,
  is_weekend BOOLEAN,
  days_before_halloween INT,
  group_size INT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP
);
